### Rothigport town Lore:

Rothigport owes much of its economic good  
fortune to its thriving port, the Dockway.  
Tradespeople from every social class do  
business throughout the Dockway district at all hours  
of the day and night, and the unfettered flow of goods  
provides Rothigport with a reputation as one of Song Tide’s  
most essential trading centers.

Rothigport is the major market town in the northern Song Tide Archipelago  Though Song Tide itself is as old as the Age of Man, Rothigport was founded about 500 januul ago. It was built on water by people who saw the water as a defense and ally. Rothigport, being one of the first seafarering people in Deluvia, built the town out in the harbor so the warring kingdoms at the time had no successful way to raid this floating town.   
It was first a dock where fisherman would come to trade hooks, nets and other equipment in the northern harbor of Goylsmuth Bay. It slowly grew over the next few hundred years as each fisherman would build a new shanty next to the last and the town cobbled together more huts and storage for their fishing industry.  This village has grown into a small city with a trading network that is now vast in Song Tide.

Recently a causeway was built connecting Rothigport to the larger island of **Noctisbard**,  to the west, called Modrik’s Causeway after the engineer who designed it. This trade route has yet to be as traveled as much as their water ways to the North and to the east but those who petitioned to build the causeway think it will become a major trade route to the rest of the islands eventually.. Sea travel is primary to the Song Tiders. Still, pilgrims, adventurers and students of the arcane walk this route on their way back and forth.

Song Tide is a fertile and diverse region so all types of beings have now settled in Rothigport, and all the warring kingdoms of the past have settled their differences and come together to grow the town. The region is also home to some magic users since it is far from the arcane-adverse Central Kingdoms. Yet, because it is a larger town, magic is kept somewhat secret, because of traveling merchants and emissaries from The Central Kingdoms might trigger a purge or war. That is to say, though there mages and wizards in Rothigport, they don’t make outward displays of magical spells and instead live out among the rural islands.

One of the reasons Rothigport survived The Great Deluge was because all of the houses are floating docks and rose with the waters.  The Goylsmuth Bay provides some protection from storms and the town founders saw to keep an open area in the center for boats to moor and dock for extra protection. The town was one of the more peaceful areas in Deluvia for a few hundred years. Only recently has crime increased because of refugees trickling in from the Central Kingdoms. The town has grown a lot in the last few decades as it is now a hub of trade for the Song Tide region. **Percimor**, the town mayor, has taken leadership and governs from his manor in the south of the harbor. Since the Deluge,, the town’s outward physical growth has mostly stopped for now, but that does not stop refugees from other areas from coming in.

Some new rumored threats have emerged to the peace-loving Rothigportians that, Druvenrog, far to the east and known for their hatred of magic, has put some of their interest toward Rothigport. Though they are too far away to pose much of a worry, there are some doomsayers in Song Tide who preach the demise of their own land.   
The rise of Necromensus and his demon clans is known but the people hope for the protection of the powerful arch mages that are known to live nearby. Many acolytes of Necromensus pray to him in shrines across Song Tide but Necromensus’ ambitions have become apparent and the strength of his magic grows.  
There are marauders and pirates who have also threatened the waters, but the pirates also do well with the trade of the town and play nice when they come to town most times. Rothigport is known as a pirate’s haven. The growth spurt of seedy taverns worries the old generation. For adventurers, they go to these locales to hear the stories and perhaps find where the next adventure awaits.  
There are many monsters who lurk in the archipelago but they keep to their own areas and rarely get close to Rothigport. The exception might be the kraken, Regnareeg, who frequents the waters just north of Rothigport.  
Because of the monsters, treasure and other adventures in Song Tide, many adventurers come to Rothigport to get provisions and hear the local rumors.

### There are the 5 Guilds of Rothigport

**Syndic of the Lumberjacks Guild**  
This Guild Is the oldest and most respected even though most foresting has declined in recent years. This industry build this town to what it is today. It is for this reason, and out of respect that stone is not used in building structures. Since the town was originally built out of wood, the strong Guild says that it will always be built out of wood. This tradition has mostly kept going.  
**Syndic of the The Shipbuilders Guild**  
One of the newer guilds that represent the emerging shipbuilders. There are two major shipbuilding companies; the Heneesri Company, House Blacktorn and the Lordiyan Builders, that latter building larger ships but fewer per yul, and the former many, many small ships every yul. This guild is them working together to protect their industry.  
**Syndic of the The Guild of Fishermen**  
An ancient guild of the fisherman, one of the oldest trades in Song Tide and powerful. All the elite in Rothigport belong to it, if only for appearances of supporting an age-honored tradition. This guild helps guard the exports and manage the tariffs.  
**Syndic of the  The Bards Guild**  
The bards are very powerful in Song Tide and commune with the powers of the wailing winds. A bard is a very desirable trait in Song Tide, but only a few are chosen to be in the guild every yul, and only a bard can be in the guild. The guild’s main purpose is to manage the lineage of the bard class and maintain its purity. This is in competition of the Sodality of Bard in Bardtown and much more rigid and systematic, looking to churn out bards to control the tides for fisherman and seafarers and to calm the storms and maelstroms. 

- Song Swellers Lodge, they use the Orinsol Ale to induce song and are very erratic. They don’t belong to any of the Bardic Halls  
- Bards of the Weeping Tide \- part of the Hall of Mischance

The moons have a big effect in the Songtide realm as they control the tides and each has their own type of herbalism and bardsong  
**Syndic of the The Arcanists Guild**  
Song Tide being haven for magic users, must have a guild representing the arcanists. Though most arch mages prefer their solitude in their own tower outside of town, many mages-in-training roam throughout Rothigport but keep a low profile. Magic is assumed to be dead by the Central Kingdoms and beings in Song Tide wish to keep it this way. This guild helps those starting out in this profession to find the necessary resources and tutelage.

There are a number of other organizations in Rothigport such as the recently founded Greenmen’s  Lodge, The Dockstayer’s Lodge

**Blackthorn Brothers**  
Thod and Igmo Blackthorn run the southeast neighborhood (sometimes derogatorily called Blackthornberg) of Rothigport . They are one of the main families in town and commissioned the main big bridge in town on the south bank of the main harbor,  to unite the east and west sides. The bridge is called the **Blackthorn Bridge**. They are vying for prestige in the town against Prigtoon. Their main trade is shipping and secretively smuggling.  
They also have been building a small force to spy on Druvvenrog. This little-known espionage guild is trying to steal information from the industrial guilds there. They currently have trade negotiations with Druvvenrog but have been smuggling goods in and out for many years.  
House Blackthorn’s colors are black and red.  
House Blackthorn’s main industry is shipping and trading. They are the second wealthiest family in Rothigport. The brothers rose up from poverty and living on the streets so they have the support of the working class, but the disdain from the Elites with which they now associate with. Though they try to enact some democratic changes, such as helping the poorer Eastsiders to cross to the wealthier west side, They have built the wealthiest neighborhood in Rothigport which is now experiencing some crime.  
Their support of the working class has helped them to become titled “Protector of the Plebs” a term of endearment and there is a rumor that they will throw their hat in the ring for the next election of the Duke. This has the other elites worried and murmurings of solutions waft through the streets.

The Anti-Tollers  
	Merki Prigtoon has proposed that there be a toll to cross the Blackthorn Bridge, so as to help pay for maintenance of the harbor and the bridges. The bridge is a symbol of equality in the city as it is what united the West Side and the East Side.The West side has been the poorer, working class which is also more religious and superstitious and the East side, though smaller, has the Guild Syndic leaders and town elites.

### Town Organization:

The town is stable in size and is considered a medium-sized city for Deluvia. It has a population of about 760, which is pretty big for anything outside the Central Kingdoms. 

#### Ethnography

* Anthoran: 48% \- one of the great races of Deluvia, though a broad group.  
* Halfling 6% \- small in stature, but clever and shrewd  
* Formori: 8% \- a group of exiles from Druverog. They came to escape the atrocities and keep their religion  
* Miliposi: 6% \- a small and blue with large ears and large eyes race. They are shrewd barters with their own district in the south east Rothigport  
* Orsi: 9% \- wise brewers of ale. They have their own religion of which their ale is a sacrament, but also their largest profit export  
* Prismarese:6% \- a partly aquatic race that is able to collect a special, valuable pearl from the deepest points in Song Tide  
* Gillaquid: 5% \- an aquatic race that lives on the bottom of the harbor but comes into town with a special land-walking-breather potion, to do business.  
* Nemedi: 5% \- A clan of exiles from Druvenrog that did not conform to the Doxy.  
* Swigtooth: 3% \- A hoofed, dirty but clever type of being that is good at bartering. They live in Rothigport   
* Elven: 2% \- A group of Kapasian exiles that broke away from the astral magic.

#### Races in the greater Song Tide that make their way into town from time to time:

* Mammramam \- The people of the swamp. They breath in the swamp gases and are able to tell the future  
* Swigtooth \- A hoofed, dirty but clever type of being that is good at bartering. They live in Rothigport   
* Swailmarkeen \- Flying creatures in the swamps. They can also dive into the water for long periods. Great fisher people.

### Economy:

Orsinowl Ale brewed by the Orsi tribe and valued by the Rothigport townspeople as the local brew.  
Fishing is the major industry in Rothigport  
Forestry and lumberjacking, though not in huge demand anymore, was the first big industry and well respected.  
Ship building is a newer industry

### Characters:

Here is some background to each character. If the NPC has stats (hp, str, magic) they are listed here.

* Duke Percimor \- Duke of Rothigport, the elected official and surrounding Goylsmuth. He and Prigtoon are in competition with each other for clout and their vision for the future of Rothigport differ. Percimor was elected as all Dukes of Rothigport have been for the past 500 years. All wishing to be Duke stand out in their boat in the harbor, and those on the docks shout the name of their favorite and try to get everyone else to shout all the same name. When one name is being shouted in unison, that person is then Duke for their life. House Percimor’s colors are yellow and black.  
* Merkti Prigtoon  \- the wealthiest merchant in Rothigport; tries to be in the affairs of everything. His house is called Ketapesh with the colors Green and Gold.  
* Majordomo Ventroth \- Prigtoon’s right hand man. Ventroth is a cleric and presides over holy affairs in Rothigport.  
* Guyhain \- an arch mage; shy and removed but willing to help the right being.  
* Derrod \- an arch mage; is secretly trying to mount an uprising against The Inquisition  
* Bufurmont \- The local reeve peacekeeper. He was assigned by Prigtoon to watch over the town market and keep weapons away. He takes his job a little too seriously and no one really takes heed of him.  
* Quinn \- the bartender at The Rusty Anchor  
* Picaroo \- a friendly pirate that tells tales in The Rusty Anchor that seem a little to big to be true.   
  Lathander \- considers himself a professional greeter. He stands outside the   
  Townhall/Fisherman Guildhall House  
  	He wants to be helpful and gives the players beginning lore information. IF it is the first time they meet him, he gives them a few wood tools, weapons and some food.

### Factions in Songtide/Rothigport:

* Muuntsatell \- The traveling sea caravan that weaves through the harbors and islands of of Songtide selling junk and treasure. The Esmerelda, is one of the boats of the caravan that broke away and is now on its own in the Long Sea.  
* Vroodic Bard Clan \- The Tide wailers of the central islands. There are many bard clans in Song Tide. They each have their own song types and instruments and unique ways of communicating. They live in a town they call Bardstown, where they practice their songspells  
* Nortide \- A seafaring elven faction that was from Kapasia, but wanted the rugged romantic life on the sea.  
* Parmite \- A clan known to harbor pirates. Their members are some of the wealthy people in Rothigport who benefit from piracy and want to keep things a bit anarchic in town.  
* Feregestine \- The diplomats that want to have the Songtide annexed into Druvenrog. Though they are too afraid to make the plea to Druvenrog themselves, they are trying to persuade others to turn with them before they do.   
* Shorgilmos \- Trouble makers, that terrorize air ships coming from the north. Potion makers of the explosive kind  
* Heneesri \- Builders of boats on the east side of Rothigport  
* Morgramel \- Magic users in hiding in the Barweeg District \- Superstitious monks that feud with unbelievers. Missionaries to the southern isles.  
* Terogweestra \- A burrowing, cavern dweller being  that live in the mines. They are excellent miners cannot come above ground without special goggles.  
* Gwrangkran \- Keepers of the molten flame. They observe and document the Volykragulon volcano passage and have a cult that worships it.  
* Trubkoyts \- Guardians of the western isles. They have an outpost in the west and bring stories back from there. They are trying to get this new area officially considered part of Song Tide, which currently it is not and considered too far away.  
* Usiatic \- A clan/cult of mountain dwellers and magic users.  
* Prismarese Waterfolk \- A being that lives mostly in the water and comes on land to hunt the skiprat. They also dive for precious materials. They have their district on the South East side of Rothigport.  
* Tongsigh \-  The bards to the Moskvrek whirlpool. Wailers of the tide  
* Hattenstawk \- Barterers on the southern coast. They make fish hooks and nets.  
* Jhumori \- desert raiders. They are magic users who hide in the The Jhumori Cliffs.

### Adventures (quests) to be had here:

**Phanasma’s Crypt**  
On the southwest side of Rothigport Port, on its own island is the Prigtoon/Ketapesh Family Mausoleum. Where Prigtoon’s daughter Phanasma, as well as other family members, are interred.

The players find rumors that she was buried with immense amounts of treasure. Phanasma was the sole child of Merkti Prigtoon and his wife Lonsa Prigtoon, of House Ketapesh of Pallamost.  
The Prigtoons are the richest family in Rothigport. Part  (most) of that money comes from the Ketapesh family and their financial interests in Rothigport from the days that House Ketapesh, one of the rival families in Pallamost, moved to Rothigport. One of their ways to keep Rothigport close was to marry one of their daughters to a rising entrepreneur in the vibrant fishing trade of this northern Song Tide region. Merkti was not a good man. He was shrewd and took every opportunity he had to advance his posture in the guilds of Rothigport and became the Syndic of the Fisherman’s Guild, one of the most prestigious posts in Rothigport. He offered many bribes to city officials and took bribes and favors himself. The highest elected official at this time, Percimor, the current Duke, was at odds with Prigtoon and kept him in check.    
Merkti hoped for an offspring so that he could teach them the ways of the markets and profits and to follow in his path and keep the family strong. It took many years, but eventually Lonsa gave birth to Phanasma. To her father’s dismay, she had no interest in industry, but he found her associating with the young magic users in the town. Her fascination with wizardry was something that Merkti did not approve of, as he felt responsible Rothigportians should boost the strength of the city through its economy, and that magic was for either the insane, or the militant.   
Phanasma defended magery and her friends and this caused many fights between her and her father. It hindered his reputation among the guilds, not that other Syndics disliked magery, on the contrary, everyone besides Merkti seemed to be on the side of the mages; but it was because of his torn relationship with his daughter. 

Phanasma would spend days away from home, and with the mages in the countryside, or in the many narrow dockstreets of Rothigport  trying to learn everything she could.

Phanasma became ill at this time of strife with her father. She had acquired Blackrot Blight (The Rot), a terrible, flesh-eating plague that is decimating populations in far off lands (The town of Hawk Finster Hollow). Merkti does not know how she contracted this but he incorrectly assumed it spread among the mage younglings because of their lack of moralsl nonetheless he was forced to quarantine her away on a tiny island near Rothigport. She is the only known case of The Rot in Rothigport so far, but is known to be spreading in other locations across Deluvia. Her personal guard Kervan, also contracted it.  
One day, Phanasma had succumbed to her illness, or so her father and many others thought. In reality, she had disappeared  Her father, Merkti, tried to cover up her disappearance by having a tomb constructed for her in the Ketapesh family catacombs just west of the city. Some townspeople think she was kidnapped. Her father, though he tries to convince everyone else that he believes she has died, has still sent out search parties for her, especially among the magic communities across Songtide, because some part of him does think she was taken away and is still alive.  
Still other devout, believe she was not really entombed but her body exhumed away to another location. 

The players will hear of the riches that are rumored to be interred with Phanasma

The quest begins on the surface, where Greer, the guard will try to deter and defend the entrance.  
The first chamber on the left is the grave of **Miss Katrina Ulvid**  
The second path to the right has Wraiths in the beginning will harass you but do little harm.  
After the wraiths is a room to the left of the crypts of The Cursed Twins, **Liza Gupp** and **Julia Gupp.** around the corner and straight is the crypt of **Phanasma Prigtoon,** and then left and straight until the tomb of **King Joe Havald**

Back starting before the wraith hall  
Up the stairs and To the left and to the left again are the graves of **Jamie Evander** and **Eleanor Evander**  
The second left has the crypt of **Alexander Holdrag** if you go straight, but then to the right is another hallway with a small table with two skulls . If you go straight up the staircase, there is a left to the crypts of **Peter Orin** and **Lyra Orin**, straight to **Randall Orin**, and right will take you to another hallway with a table with two skulls. If you take a right down the stairs and then a right, there is one room on the left for the crypts of **Eris Stonehar**t and **Launa Stonehar**t, then the rest is a dead end.  
 a left from the steps, the first room on the right is the crypt of **Panza**. Further down is a dead end after table and skulls, a left that goes down a hall. A room on the right is the crypts of **Aldis Richmond** and **Lyris Richmond**, and further down that hall way is one last crypt to the left of **Sarun Lassis**

To the left is the crypts of **Richard Lavander** and **Josefine Lavander**

**The cursed twins** 

The players will get an item and a clue from each of the crypts. After they visit each crypt each crypt summons an Unburied, which they must fight to get the item. When they defeat the Unbured, the Unburied’s soul can be put to rest.  
they will be able to conjure the **Sedladus** , the old architect of the catacombs and managed the interment of many of the residents; in the final room. He was accidentally sealed upon the completion of the tombs and none of the gravediggers knew what happened to him. He became undead. They must also get the key to the door by fighting the Cursed Twins

The second half of this adventure is a secret cult has taken up residence in further tunnels below the crypts if the players can find them. This cult is the Keepers of the Book of Bones  
The caved-in  old entrance at the bottom. It leads to a very old Ossuary where a cult has taken as their meeting quarters. No one can get through this cave in except through secret ways. The Bone Church, as the stories go, and haunted stories told to Song Tider children to keep them in line, is a humongous cathedral below ground with a labyrinth of tunnels.  
The Bone Church, also designed by Sedladus, made entirely of bone. His designs drove him mad in trying to perfect them, which caused his neglectful passion to complete the project, when his workers accidentally sealed him in. It is said that he completed his design in his remaining starved days etching the blueprint and notes of his masterpiece into the stone floor of the antechamber with his bloody fingernails and until his digits were mere nubs. This glorious tribute would be to **Ossidarius the Bone Father** when finished. It never was, but what was completed is more than adequate for the Keepers of the Book of Bones, who wish to bring Ossidarius back among the pantheon of Song Tide, and even all of Deluvia, if only they can find an architect to finish Sedladus’ vision. His walking corpse may provide some clues, as it haunts the antechamber that is blocked at the bottom of the Rothcrest Crypts.

The players goal in the catacombs could be to get some treasure. There is treasure from the graves, from the monsters, and from Phanasma’s grave.  
They also can find out that

The tomb of the Soldier Kervan  
Kervan was the loyal guard of the Ketapesh House when they first came to Rothigport  
He was fiercely protective of Lonsa as he part of the Pallatian Guard before their disbandment during the dissolution of Pallamost. When Phanasma was born, he guarded her and helped raise her, especially in training her in mastery of arms. When Phanasma was in exile, he was the only one to stay with her to protect her. Prigtoon ordered that he stay at his post to guard the family and its coffers but he insisted that he stay with her. When he contracted “The Rot”, Prigtoon then conceded. When they both succumbed to the illness Kervan was laid not far from Phanasma in the family tomb. His tomb is sealed with a copper lock. The key is located in the the crypt of Kervan’s squire, Panza, his trusty shieldbearer assistant. Panza fell into depression after Kervan’s death and only outlasted him for a few years in solitude and squalor and sour spirits  
Panza lis in unrest as all the corpses in the Crypt do based on the many distress of Phanasma’s ordeal and because of the haunting by Sedladus. Panza wants to help the players get into Kervan’s tomb

Riddle ideas  
In darkness, I lie with the dead, forgotten by all but the restless. Seek out the bones of those who came before, and you may find the key to what lies hidden.

Beneath the surface, buried deep, lies the secrets of the long forgotten keep. The Ossuary hidden from sight, only those who solve the riddle can shed light.

Among the bones of the past, lies the key to unlocking the door that lasts. Seek out the clues and follow the signs, and the hidden Ossuary you'll soon find.

"In the catacombs, where bones lie deep, a secret waits for those who seek. Look to the past and find the key, and you'll unlock the mystery."

"Among the shadows and the bones, a hidden chamber waits alone. The past will guide you to the door, and secrets will be yours to explore."

**"Amidst the crypts and endless halls, lies a place few have seen at all. Seek out the bones of those long gone, and you'll find the way to carry on."**

"Beneath the earth and out of sight, a chamber waits for those with might. The bones of kings and paupers alike, will lead you to the prize you seek."

Katrina Ulvid’s room:  
I was once the matriarch of a great name,  
A legacy of power, wealth, and fame.  
But now I rest within this tomb,  
A silent memory of my doom.

My family's legacy lives on,  
But my spirit cannot move beyond.  
If you can find the key that's lost,  
My soul will pay the final cost.

The players must find a key

OR

I am a ghost, without a doubt,  
A riddle I have, to figure it out.

What is it that remains when all is done?  
A residue left, after the burning's begun.

It's not quite fire, nor quite soot,  
But a substance that's often overlooked.

Some say it's dark, some say it's white,  
But it's the same substance, day and night.

So tell me, traveler, can you see  
What is the answer to my riddle for thee?

Answer is ASH

What was once alive, now lays still,  
Reduced to remnants of its will.  
A grayish powder, dull and fine,  
What once was bright, has now declined.

ASH

Or 

I am the master of destruction,  
My power is feared by all without exception.  
With a touch I can end a life,  
Or lay waste to everything in sight.  
From the dirt I rise, a force of rage and light,  
Conquering all with my intense might

The cursed twins room:  
Twins we were, but now we're two,  
Cursed to be forever anew.  
Our bones may rest beneath this stone,  
But our spirits roam, forever alone.

Look closely and you'll see our mark,  
A symbol of our eternal dark.  
Find the key to break the curse,  
Or join us in this endless hearse

The answer to this riddle could be a hidden symbol or carving that the adventurers need to find to unlock a secret compartment or door. Alternatively, the key could be a magical amulet or artifact that has the power to break the curse and free the spirits of the twins. The curse itself could be something like a perpetual cycle of death and rebirth or being trapped between worlds, which the adventurers need to unravel in order to break it.

Or 

In life we were as one, inseparable and strong,  
But now in death, we're bound in agony so long.  
Cursed we were by a wicked spell,  
Trapped forever in this dark, dank cell.

Our names once echoed through the halls,  
But now we're just forgotten souls in these walls.  
If you can break the curse that binds us here,  
Our spirits will be free from fear.  
The answer to this riddle could be a series of steps or clues that the adventurers must follow to break the curse on the twins. This could involve finding and using certain objects in the crypt, or performing a specific ritual to break the curse. The curse could be tied to the larger narrative of the puzzle adventure, and the twins may hold some key piece of information or object that the adventurers need to progress.

To break the curse:  
Find the Twins' tombstones in the crypt and light a candle on each one.

Place a lock of hair from each of the twins in a bowl of water, along with a sprig of rosemary and a pinch of salt.

Recite the following incantation:

"By the power of earth, air, fire, and sea,  
Break this curse and set us free.  
Twins cursed in life and death,  
Hear our plea and take a breath.  
Rise up from your darkened tomb,  
And let your spirits leave this room."

Pour the water onto the ground and wait for a sign from the spirits of the Cursed Twins.

If the curse is truly broken, the spirits of the twins should be at peace and may offer some guidance or assistance to the adventurers. If the curse is not broken, the twins may appear in a more menacing form, and the adventurers will have to find another way to escape the crypt.

The truth about The Rot, is that it is plague magic, a type of Death magic, that comes from Wraithwood, The Death Lord, Necromensus, was always jealous of the power his grandchildren received by working with the mortals and of the Fae of the wood

The start of the Rot in the center of Faewood, just north of The Valley of the Moon. Because of the power of the Tree it had to move northward and overtook all it came in contact with. The edge of it is called the Rotted Reach, or The Northern Reach, since it is moving northward. It overtook the Well Tree and corrupted the tree’s form and is now the home of one of the Lich Kings and in the center of Wraithwood.  
The first mortals The Rot came in contact with were a group of lumberjacks from the town of Hawk Finster Hollow. They contracted the plague and brought it back to the town which is currently under its affliction.

**Moskvrek** the maelstrom \- swallower of ships. It has been said that if a ship can get close enough and harpoon the maw of Moskvrek there is great treasure to be found. No ship has lived to tell the tale.

**The Sea Hag** \- witch of songtide inner sea

**Termir Mograg**  
Termir is a mage is in the SE of Song Tide, in the Geistgor Mountains. He believes the mages should embrace technology and has put it upon himself to use both magic and technology. He has built his own airship which is partly powered by magic. He is the leader of this movement to use magic to power vessels which is very experimental and not trusted by most in Song Tide  
He is at 1933, 200,  He is not part of the Four arch mages because he wants to do his own thing. Although he is as powerful as the Four Archmages, he is solitary and chooses to go his own way.

Magistus the Wise  is a powerful sorcerer with incredible abilities and also the keeper of the Magic Forest. His Bookstore contains some of the rarest books in the world. He is also the wisest man on Deluvia and people from everywhere come to his store to seek answers but they all get told \- “Your answer is in this book”. Then he hands them one of his books and tells them to go in the Reading Cage and stay there until they find their answers. The more they read, the wiser he gets as the magic flows throughout the pages. Once they finish it, they return the book and leave the place with a sense of gratitude and relief, for they have found their answers. 

## The Four Archmages of the Song Tide

The magic lines that run through the are of Deluvia by the Song Tide Archipelago are strong, and it is why the Arch Mages have found their home here for as long as our history was written.  
They are powerful wielders of spells, but they keep their magic to a minimum in the current age, as there are the rumors of Druvenrog’s will to quell the use of magic in all of Deluvia. The four of them provide a protective force around the islands that make their presence less known to all, especially Druvenrog and those that seek to harm them.

**Nax Hollum** \- The Arch Mage of the Magery Guild.   
He is one of the founders of the town of Rothigport, which makes him 486 years old. An Anthoran of the Owl-clan sub-species. He lost one eye in the Battle of Egot Deletholl during the War of the Third Age against the gods. He fought alongside Aldvader Grimstok for the glory of the mortals but split ways after the wars, and when Aldvader gave into the dark forces of the Nemedi Druvs.  
His colors are white and aqua blue  
His manor is called Raxelcroft Keep which is just southeast of Rothigport  
Nax fled the Central Kingdoms and settled in Song Tide. Nax believed in the power of potions of magic more than the potions of herbs  
makes potions for the player . He is called just a crazy superstitious old man by much of Rothigport. He is also the stuff of bedtime stories to the children to scare them.  
	Located just southeast of Rothigport  
	Song Tide    /tppos 924 206 513  
	Nax has an apprentice in Rothigport named Rosage. Rosage is also the town scribe and has a large library of Rothigportian books.  
Rosage keeps an eye for what is going on in Rothigport and reports it Nax, since Nax, like most old mages, likes to stay out of the fray of daily life.  
Nax won’t see the players until they have visited Rosage and helped Rosage with his potion reagents gathering quest.  
Being a master of Wind Magic (aeromancy), Nax, can

**Reg Therox**  
	Song Tide    is located on the Chantwood Isle and can be reached in Minwood Snag, if one travels up the snag to the top, and follows the cave then the path to his roost.  
He is sparrow clan and lives in his tree roost library.

	He is in east central Song Tide deep in the forest at a hidden lake. He controls the water flow from the **Dreglemat River** and is in commune with the **Dreglematical Turg**, a spirit of that river and lake. His home is a tall water tower that can be filled. A player can manipulate the water levels to gain access to certain regions of Song Tide.

**Orta Vollim** \- Ward of Southern Approach (near the volcano)  
Song Tide    /tppos \-223 127 2879  
She is on the very southern side of what is known as the Song Tide Archipelago, She seeks solace and a place to commune with  the sea. The boost in pilgrimages to the nearby Temples  have given her less solitude, but she still does not mind helping pilgrims find their way.

The four mages together offer a Large quest to the player. 

Every mage in Song Tide can teach spells, but the Four Arch Mages can help the player learn to craft their own spells

How to craft spells

Need components and reagents and inscription and magery

TRIGGER

TARGET

**Area** \- Targets all units in a radius from the current target   
	Radius, Through Wall,  \# of Targets, Randomize Targets?  
**Cone** \- Targets all units in a line in front of the current target   
Angle, Range, Through Wall, \# of Targets,  
**Linear** \- Targets all units in a line in front of the current target   
	Range, Tolerance (how wide the cone),  through wall, max targets  
**Location** \- Targets the reticle location of the target or caster. Combine this with another targeting type for ranged area effects.  
	Range  
**Nearest** \- Targets the closest unit(s) in a radius from the current target  
Radius, Max targets  
**Single \-** Targets a single unit in front of the current target	  
	Range,,  
	NOTES: This one uses the Denizen “shoot” command, so it cannot go through wall

**Self** \- yourself

The higher the magery, the lower the mana cost, cooldown, buildup and damage  
The higher the inscription, the better success in crafting  
The components determine which spell is created

Dragon's Blood: A powerful substance often used to amplify the potency of spells and potions.  
Siren's Tears: A rare and precious substance, known for its ability to enhance spells related to emotions and persuasion.  
Phoenix Feather: Known for its ability to enhance spells related to rebirth and renewal.  
Basilisk Venom: Employed in spells to induce fear or petrification, as well as in antidotes for particularly potent curses.  
Mandrake Root: Used for its potent healing properties and its ability to amplify the effects of restorative spells.  
Glowing Mushrooms: Known for their luminescent properties, they are used in spells related to illumination and enlightenment.  
Eye of Newt: Frequently employed in concoctions for its ability to enhance perception and foresight.  
Fairy Dust: Often used to add a touch of enchantment and allure to spells, enhancing their overall effectiveness.  
Wolfsbane: Known for its power in protection spells and its ability to ward off evil spirits and curses.  
Unicorn Horn: A versatile reagent that can be used in various spells, including those related to purity and protection.  
Moonstone Dust: Gathered under the light of a full moon, it's used for enhancing spells related to intuition and dreamwork.  
Ethereal Hummingbird Feathers: Gifted by otherworldly messengers, they are utilized in spells for swift transformation and transcendence.  
Lunar Quartz Crystals: Known for their calming energy, they are used in spells to enhance intuition and promote emotional balance.  
Labyrinthine Ivy: Found in mystical mazes, it's used for spells related to uncovering secrets and unlocking hidden knowledge.  
Starlight Essence: Captured during celestial alignments, it's known for its ability to infuse spells with cosmic energy and insight.  
Sighing Breeze Essence: Gathered at the crossroads of elemental planes, it's known for its ability to evoke emotions and inspire change.  
Enchanted Silver Thread: Woven by skilled artisans under magical conditions, it's used for spells related to binding and protection against dark forces.  
Dancing Flame Essence: Extracted from the heart of eternal flames, it's utilized in spells to ignite passion and creativity.  
Echoing Seashells: Found on distant shores, they are utilized in spells that amplify the power of spoken words and incantations.  
Timeless Sands: Collected from elusive hourglasses hidden in forgotten realms, they are used in spells for manipulating time and destiny.  
Moonlit Dew: Collected from plants at night, it's used for spells related to enhancing intuition and dream interpretation.  
Feathered Whispers: Gathered from birds known for their symbolic meanings, they're used in spells for guidance and protection.  
Silver Thorns: Found on certain plants, they're utilized for protection spells and to ward off negative energy.  
Labyrinth Moss: Grown in winding patterns, it's used for spells related to journeys, both physical and spiritual.  
Whispering Crystals: Small, enchanted crystals known for their ability to enhance communication and divination.  
Astral Wind Whisper: Captured during gentle breezes on clear nights, it's used in spells to enhance perception and connection to the universe.  
Wandering Fireflies: Captured and released during specific phases of the moon, they're used to add an element of enchantment to spells.  
Eternal Flame Resin: Extracted from candles that have burned for extended periods, it's used to ignite passion and willpower.  
Mystic Runes: Inscribed with ancient symbols, they serve as a focus for divination and scrying.  
Time-Touched Sand: Collected from special beaches with unique sand colors, it's used in time-related spells and rituals.  
Silver Fern Leaves: Found in forest groves, they are used for spells related to luck and protection.  
Enigmatic Moonflower Petals: Blooming under moonlight, they are used in spells that enhance intuition and psychic awareness.  
Dew of the Morning Petal: Collected at sunrise, it's utilized in spells for revitalization and new beginnings.  
Sparkling River Pebbles: Gathered from meandering streams, they are known for their use in spells related to clarity and emotional balance.  
Twilight Moss: Gathered at dusk, it's known for its ability to enhance spells that bridge the gap between day and night.  
Whispering Oak Bark: Harvested from ancient trees, it's utilized in spells for grounding and connecting with the natural world.  
Echoing Quartz Crystals: Sourced from deep caverns, they are used for spells related to amplifying energy and intention.  
Soothing Chamomile Buds: Found in sunlit fields, they are used for spells related to relaxation and emotional healing.  
Tranquil Pond Water: Collected from serene waters, it's utilized in spells for calming and soothing troubled emotions.  
Emberwood Ash: Derived from sacred bonfires, it's known for its use in spells related to transformation and renewal.  
Amber Resin: Utilized for its grounding and protective properties, often used in spells for stability and clarity.  
Fey Wildflower Nectar: Harvested from enchanted meadows, it's utilized in spells that promote healing and harmony.  
Silver Moon Dew: Collected under moonlight, it's known for enhancing spells related to intuition and feminine energy.  
Stardust Essence: Gathered under the night sky, it's known for enhancing spells related to wishes and aspirations.  
Frostbloom Petals: Found in snowy landscapes, they are used for spells that invoke the energies of winter and purification.  
Whispering Wind Seeds: Carried by gentle breezes, they are utilized in spells for communication and fostering connections.  
Solar Ash: Gathered at sunrise, it's utilized in spells that harness the energy of the sun and promote vitality and strength.  
Ember Moss: Found in the heart of ancient forests, it's used in spells to ignite passion and creativity.  
Wisp Willow Wood: Collected from ancient willow trees, it's used for spells related to intuition and fluidity of emotions.

Each component has aspects which can determine the spells usage.  
1 is its power, such as change, cause, negate, etc  
2 is the target, such as single, linear, area of effect, etc  
3 is the elemental effect, such as fire damage

To inscribe a spell, you need some vellum, a quill and at least four components. The four components will randomly generate a spell based on the aspects of them. One of the components is randomly picked to drop from the algorithm

Once the spell is crafted. It can be put into your spellbook to use forever. Or you could sell the scroll to someone else and not be able to use other. Thirdly, you could use the scroll, for a one time use, at a success rate of 100%, but an assured delay of 2 seconds.

### The Emerald Bracelet:

/warp wasteland  
/rg wasteland\_isle

The Mage Ildar **Timistrius** lives in the far off isle known as The Wasteland (aka **Ildaria** when it was beautiful). She is in an awful mood because nothing will grow on her realm.  She believes this is because her magic is waning  and finds out that her gardener is also failing her in his tasks.   
She would like the player to find her a new gardener, or find some new magic that will restore her realm into a lush garden as it once was.  
The player finds out through talking with some Rothigport’s townspeople that **Rinkelspeare**, the faerie trickster of **Rystrilmyl**, out of jealousy, has stolen Timistrius’ gardener, whose songs are the source of the once flourishing gardens growth. The gardener, is a Tree Ent from Fecundia who has been taught in the ways of turgorimancy (*Turgorimancy* in Deluvic, *Life magic* in common tongue),  and knows the sing spell of **Anternacantus**  (*Anternacantus* in Deluvic or *Song Life* in the common tongue) ( a bard spell to cause plants to grow or mega fauna to behave a certain way). The gardener, **Frondo**, sings things song spells while doing his gardening duties, making some of the most wonderful gardens in the realm.

Erino

### The Mawg Witch 

**The Mawg Witch** has a hut in the **Rystrilmyl**, and offers tools to help gather the pollen and fruit from the mega flora in Rystrilmyl.  She also instructs the player on how to subdue Mandragor in order to obtain the root.

She will give the player The Charm of Mawg 

### Mandragora

Mandragora is the root beast of the wild lands, The Mandrake Queen. Located to the south of Song Tide she rests underground waiting for fauna to pass by. Her roots sprout little plants that come to the surface that many naturalists seek for their medicinal attributes of pain relief, strength giving and euphoric properties. These plants, which are children of Mandragora, have been highly sought and are rare among Deluvia, because they are found in this one spot, and they are dangerous to gather. If Mandragora awakens, the gatherer will likely be swallowed into the dirt and strangled in her roots.

Ancient rumors exist that she once walked Deluvia with her roots as legs and arms but and distributing strength to all; but was cursed by the waters of Wraithwood which caused her retreat and shriveling back deep into the soil.

Many seekers of magic reagents look for Mandragora’s resting spot for this root. She resists having her children taken away.

### Rystrilmyl

Is an area in western Song Tide, that is bewitched by **Finnwyl**. Finnwyl is the demi-goddess that resides in central Song Tide and exerts her bidding over the general area. There is a temple that worships her in Omphalos, the very center of Deluvia (so called), but she has a particular interest in Rystramyl and has given extra-ordinary imbuement of life force into the tree of Rystralonyan (In the tongue of the Gods, *Drasil* means Magic wood; and *nyan* means Gifted). A faerie-folk, **Rinkelspeare**,  lives in Rystralonyan and is somewhat of a trickster but remains in the favor of Finnwyl. Rystralonyan was gifted by nemistri to Finnwyl, her sister, to solidify their alliance. Finnwyl took pride in the Rastrilonyan Tree, and Rystramyl and bewitched the small area and now mega fauna and mega flora grow there unlike anywhere else in Deluvia.

These flora have pollen that can be gathered by players for all sorts of purposes. Every day these flora appear in new places in Rystrilmyl. They cannot be spawned outside Rystrilmyl.

The Dendroot is the base of the tree, that leads to the Urd Drasil

**Migreelamyre** \- the swamp to the south of Rystralonyan and part of Rystrilmyl
