# Frostwynn Lore 

History About The Lady of the Snow  
In the Age of Gods, Boralumugheil, cast the land in darkness, frost and hibernation to keep his daughter, Embreas from being courted by Necromensus for they were at war with each other. Necromensus and Embreas were still wed and their daughter Freymiss was born to grow and bring the end of the hibernation by killing her grandfather, Boralumugheil. As he lay in her arms, from her grief and guilt she shed a tear that became frozen and as it fell to the frozen ground, broke into three shards. Before Boralumugheil died, his blood fused with the tears passing on some of his power of light and dark. The shards sat on the ground and when the ground melted from the new spring, they each grew into a flower. Freymiss went into exile.  
During the Age of Man, 3 of the 12 Sages, during their wanderings, came across the flowers, and each picked and took one for themselves. When they found their resting place and planted the flowers, they bloomed into women. Each of the 3 women took the 3 Sages for their husband. They were Falthori, Seydna, and Calnora.  
Falthori married The Free Spirit begat Charn, Bristor, Epleyna  
Seydna married The Transformer begat Seritipi, Finnwyl, Nemistri  
Calnora married The Scholar  begat  Malfisis, Dalmisis, Brumisis

From all of these were born the beings that would become the Age of Kings. All the children rose to greatness at some point but it was Seritipi whose realm held over to the age of mortals.

Another note is that Boralumugheil’s wife is Sophgritus comes from the southern jungle lands and is goddess of the winds, which is why her children are now keepers of that trait. Finnwyl, her granddaughter, went to Sophgritus’ homelands and now occupies the Jungle Temple, the center of the world, and where the gods met the first mortals (purportedly by those that live there and follow Finnwyl). Nemistri holds power at the Tree of the Wood, and Finnwyl of the center of Song Tide, but much of their power has been relinquished to the Age of Kings.

Seritipi remains the most powerful of these demi-gods from the North. Nemistri, is a close second, and Finnwyl the third, Seritipi is most powerful because of Frostwyn slows down memory, and by her taking rule there, the memory of the Age of Gods is stronger (less dissipated). 

Current time:

**Seritipi** is The Lady of the Snow. She is part god, part mortal, part witch, part demon. She inherited the blood of her great-grandfather Boralumugheil, whom she wishes to return to greatness. She also has some of the goodness of her grandmother, but some the deviousness of Necromensus in her veins. Her realm was one that was created during the Age of the Gods, but still persists today. In her realm, many of the secrets of the Age of the Gods can be found, as they are frozen in time in fragments throughout Frostwyn. The one area that has been infiltrated is by Bokmal and the Frost Trolls in east Frostwyn, that is to say, this area is not truly under her rule, though probably could be if she willed it enough.

In the beginning part of the quest, the player will learn about the above, and this knowledge will help them gain access to her inner domain, including her fortress, **Mollbrufrost**. Seritipi is not evil nor wants to hurt the players, but would like to seduce them into helping her regain greatness for her lineage; mostly against Necromensus. There are plenty of dangerous events to harm the players in the realm, but Seritipi’s method is to sway them through charm and to enchant them into become part of her Ice Spectre army. She does have plans to rise against Necromensus, her grandfather, since she sides with Boralumugheil and would not mind seeing Necromensus fall down a few pegs, since his power and land is also gaining and becoming a threat to all kingdoms.

### **Other Quests of Frostwynn**

* Possess the  **Horolymventus** \- **Kitherin** The Sage the Free Spirit’s Clock of the Winds  
  * Sage the Free Spirit lives on the southern edge of Frostwynn on an island. His castle is actually a large Orrery of gears and planets called **DreamHelm**. Being the embodiment of the free spirit that is unique to the mortal races, he explores the the celestial bodies around Deluvia through a special aetheric spells that is channelled through his orrery. Dreamhelm is also the channel for the hand held device of the Horolymventus. The Horolymventus, when held by   
  * Antukitherus \- another device invented by Kitherin  
* Sage the Aggressor recruitment into the Resistance against Druvenrog  
* Bokmal and the Ice Trolls  
* Brumaltus’ puzzles and requests that you descend into the deep Well of frozen souls to recover his diamonds.  
* Assemble the Borastercleave \- this is an epic axe that is first found in the Mullbrufrost Castle, but then can be amended with amazing gems from Frostwynn  
* Uniting the Goblins \-  Although this quest can be initiated in many parts of Deluvia, much of it takes place in Frostwynn. The Goblins are a race spread apart across Deluvia. Some factions wish to be reunited under the original goblin king, Aleighgazor 

### **The main quest of Frostwynn**

### Part I \- The Lore of Frostwynn

The player first learns about The Lady of the Snow from one of the following:  1.) Herrothorg prison, 2.) her sister in the Jungle Temple, 3.) from Bokmal, 4.) nemistri of the Wood or, 5.)  from The Sage The Consumer  
The player must first wander the Frostwyn searching for artifacts in the ice shards which give more tips into the Age of the Gods, which can lead to other quests about the Gods and unlock special power from Gods. 

Her fortress shows up seemingly in different places across Frostwyn each sunrise, so it’s hard for the players to find. The player can happen to stumble upon it, or find the system which it uses to decide where it will appear. It uses the Frost Winds (from which Frostwyn gets it name), as a sort of clock/compass to determine its location. The 8 Winds of the North (The Frost Winds), cross the ice plains in different directions. Each wind is controlled by an old god, one of Boralumugheil children Samaurora (note: Seritipi’s Grandmother), Brumetheus, Tijirimal, Boraminimus, Zruniphor, Tulehadihud,  Drangameen and Sevri, as they blow across the plains their frigid breath. Each takes turns being the most powerful for that day and The Free Spirit Sage has made a clock map to determine the order in which this occurs. There are 32 possible locations The Lady of the Snow’s fortress can appear. Through clues, the player learns of this and then can seek The Free Spirit Sage for the map. This is another free-standing large quest with rewards and perils of its own. The Free Spirit has long since moved far away, so this is a long voyage, but can save the player some time to learn the location of the fortress or they can use luck to randomly find it. They can only enter during the day, between sunrise and sunset, for at night, it is ethereally traveling to its new location.

Frostwyn is a wide and vast ice plain with some ice mountains and boreal forest. It is mostly uninhabited except for the Frost Trolls to the east, and other monsters; and the very south west corner, which was colonized by New Pallamost. New Pallamost had some failed towns there, but now just has a large prison there, called Herrothorg. Through Herrothorg, is the most common way to get to Frostwyn, as once imprisoned there, prisoners will hear about the story of the Lady of the Snow, and why escape is futile, because either the weather will get them, or the Lady of the Snow will freeze them into a pillar of ice. The latter is not true, merely a fable, but keeps the prisoners afraid of escaping (though some of The Lady’s  minions might freeze them\!)  
The reason for her fortress moving randomly is to seek the frozen blood of her great-grandfather, Boralumugheil and use it in a ritual to bring him back and return his greatness back to Frostwynn. She is obsessed with this and keeping the power of Necromensus’ power at a minimum. Before Boralumugheil’s death, during the early part of the Age of the Gods, all of Deluvia was covered in ice by his power for an eon, and when he died, the ice has since retreated to what is now, only Frostwyn.

Rewards to be had before getting to The Lady of the Snow are some wind magic from the 8 gods. There are 8 spells to learn, one from each. The 8 Frost Winds are in the 8 corners of Frostwyn, though not hard to find, they are quite a distance apart.

Samaurora \- unleash freezing gail  
Brumetheus \- the bringer of blizzard   
Tijirimal \- Lord of frostbite  
Boraminimus \- Freezer of souls  
Zruniphor \- The winter bringer  
Tulehadihud \- queen of hail  
Drangameen \- The slower of memories  
Sevri \- Wind of parched chill

Each of these Winds is a mini-dungeon, that must be solved and navigated to find the end Wind god and get one of the spells. Each will give a clue to the player to help find The Free Spirit (now far away) and gain his clock. They will each give a clue to how to solve a certain room in The Lady of the Snow’s fortress.

There are the 14 artifacts embedded in shards of ice that are remnants of the Age of the Gods. Each unlocks some lore and 12 of them unlock a new language fragment to learn the ancient Deluvic language. The 12 Sages each unlock another 12 language fragments, and the remaining 12 are scattered throughout Deluvia. The reason a good portion of them are in Frostwyn, is because this land is mostly untouched and preserved as when the Gods were first humiliated. The Ancient Deluvic is a complicated runic language, but can help the player solve many other ancient riddles in the world, and tap into power words, the clerics can find very useful since it is the language first used by mortals and that which most closely resembles the Tongue of the Gods.  
All 14 of the Frostwynn shards has an artifact of power that can help the player in Deluvia.

Each shard must be brought back to the Great Forge, in the depths of Druvenrog to be melted since they are frozen with frost magic and can only be melted with the heat of the center of Deluvia.  They are scattered around in many different locations and are hard to find, many times, buried deep in the ice.

Shard 1: 	**Agurn Talisman**  \-   
		A fragment of the Deluvic Stone language  
		A piece of lore of the old gods  
Shard 2:	**Divi’s Orb**  \-  Divi, a netharic goddess, lost her orb of Enlightenment, which was   
		stolen by Necromensus and dropped here during one of his courtings of    
		Embreas. This orb was Divi’s way of bringing to real truth to the netharic   
		people and relieving them of their shackles  
A fragment of the Deluvic Stone language  
		A piece of lore of the old gods  
Shard 3: 	**Malfisis’ Shard** \- reveals more about his cousin, The Lady of the Snow’s history  
		A fragment of the Deluvic Stone  
		A piece of lore of the old gods  
		1/3rd of The *Blade of Abhorrence*  
Shard 4:	**Daltisis’ Shard** \- reveals more about his cousin, The Lady of the Snow history  
		A fragment of the Deluvic Stone   
		A piece of lore of the old gods  
		1/3rd of The *Blade of Abhorrence*  
Shard 5:	**Brumisis’ Shard** (note: no language fragment)  \- reveals more about his cousin,   
		The Lady of the Snow’s history  
		A piece of lore of the old gods  
		1/3rd of The *Blade of Abhorrence*  
Shard 6:	**Miningua’s Ambition** \- a stone tablet telling of the war that started the  
		Humiliation of the Gods \- When held, grants commune with the Sage,   
The Aggressor for advice in conquest in war. Starts the quest of becoming a   
	General in the resistance army (as a sub-profession)  
\- A fragment of the Deluvic Stone   
Shard 7: 	**Boralumugheil’s Blood** \- (note: no language fragment) \- This is what The Lady   
		Of the Snow is looking for. Bring it to her to skip a whole large section of her   
		fortress and gain her favor at court, or the player can keep it for themself to do a   
		number of things, such as damage Necromensus, or free the Ice Spectres back   
		Into the corporeal realm. This is one of the most powerful shards and should not   
		be easy to attain.  
Shard 8:	**Permafrost mushrooms** \- Eat to provide extra protection from frost damage OR,   
		Present to the Delvwitch, deep in The Lady’s fortress, to make the Delvwitch your 		ally in fighting the Lady’s henchman, Murobrontz, the Snow Laputaur.   
		\-A fragment of the Deluvic Stone   
Shard 9:	**Ninnybruck Maps** \- a map of the passes in the WildStorms, the thick storm   
		clouds that surround Deluvia, granting access to the Aethersphere. Called the   
Ninnybruck maps after Gearheed Ninnybruck the first explorer of the skies and who crashed and died presumably at this location. Some locations, such as Northtop are known passes, but there are others, that no one knows about which could be geo-strategic points  
\-A fragment of the Deluvic Stone   
Shard 10:	**Krallthroy’s Torch** \- A torch that can melt many ice creatures in the realm. Can   
		also process/melt Felluvian Ice. Prevents or slows frost damage  
		\-A fragment of the Deluvic Stone  
		\-A piece of lore of the old gods  
		\- Chalice of Aminubith \- a potion of warming  
Shard 11: 	**Frozen Ichor** \- ancient dragon blood, provides power beyond belief, but must first  
		Consult or become  a technopriest to wield  
		\-A fragment of the Deluvic Stone  
		\-A piece of lore of the old gods  
Shard 12:	**Xandrius Cellar Key** \- a key to a special room in the Library of Xandrius in   
		New Pallamost.   
		\-A fragment of the Deluvic Stone  
		\-A piece of lore of the old gods  
Shard 13: 	**Wolfsbane** \- many medicinal and poisonous properties depending on the user.   
		Can also damage werewolves. Must first learn Zruniphor’s wind spell to find   
		Instead of bringing to The Great Forge.  
		\-A fragment of the Deluvic Stone  
		\-A piece of lore of the old gods  
Shard 14:	**Felluvian Ice** \- The cure to the plague, and a rare ingredient in many air-faring   
		implements, otherwise only found in the Aethersphere gas realm (one of the   
		three essential gases hunted in the aethersphere, the others being   
		Rhodenite, Chlorodyne. )  
		\-A fragment of the Deluvic Stone  
		\-A piece of lore of the old gods

Three of Lady of the Snow’s cousins have stayed back in Frostwyn (Malfisis, Dalmisis, and Brumisis), and guard 3 of the artifacts and claim to be guardians of them, though they are merely menacing tricksters. The interesting thing is that each of these shards (besides other rewards they give) can be combined into the *Blade* of Abhorrence, well worth the price of dueling these petty demi-demons.

More ice spells can be learned from various casters in Frostwyn. Bokmal and the ice trolls have their own flavor of ice magic that they would be happy to use on the player before teaching it, See that quest.

Various ice weapons, armor and devices can be found. New ice/snow-type monsters can be found to fight. 

The players must learn how to enter the fortress after they learn where it will appear. There is a special key, the Hailstone crystal, which when placed in the headstone of the statue of the Queen of Hail on the eastern edge of the fortress, opens  a gate. The Hailstone crystal lies far to the north on a small island surrounded by frigid waters where the player must solve Brumaltus’ puzzles (another separate quest) and descend into the deep Well of frozen souls to recover Brumaltus’ diamonds.

### Part II \- The Ice Fortress of Mollbrufrost

Once in the Fortress, on the first level there are 8 rooms, one for each of the Winds that the player must solve. If the player has sought the Eight Frost Winds previously. They can use that certain spell and the advice given by the Frost Wind God to solve the room. If the player is not a mage, they get a wand with the spell embedded with a certain amount of charges.

LEVEL 1 \-   
Room 1:  Freeze spell \- the player must manipulate ice columns to get through a maze  
Room 2:  Blizzard spell \- the player causes a blizzard in the room which causes the causes drifts and switches around the contents of the room to open new entrances. This also causes snow blindness to enemies.  
Room 3: Frostbite spell \- withers all mortal (enemy) beings in the room with frost damage  
Room 4: Hibernation spell \- put enemies into long sleep  
Room 5: Bring the solarium to winter, killing the creeping plants  
Room 6: Hail damage to dissolve iron blocks and rearrange room to reveal new secrets  
Room 7: Slowing memory \- This room allows you to alter future levels and the puzzles to come. It also provides a potion of memory slowing which can be given to the Lady’s messenger which can be later used to confuse messages passed from and to The Lady to other kingdoms.  
Room 8: Shatter the ice in the room and lower the temperature, killing all non-frost creatures (including the player if they don’t have Frost protection, they should have some sort of frost protection before entering this room)

LEVEL 2  
Murobrontz, the Snow Laputaur, a miniboss. If they have first met and appeased the Delvwich, she helps fight Murobrontz. Murobrontz is a huge lion head with horse body creature that lives in the snow and helps The Lady keep Frostwyn under her command by doing her bidding. He is weakened by fire damage and further by the Delvwich curse.   
When defeated, Murobrontz drops his battle axe, The **Borastercleave**, which can be picked up, an ancient frost dwarf artifact. Murobrontz also accepts his fate but asks to be slain by his battle axe so that he may enter the afterlife (Halsingreevs, the resting place of frost megafauna warriors) as a true warrior of the Frost winds. If the player accepts and uses the axe, he will put in a good word for the player in Halsingreevs. This blessing opens up quests to imbue Borastercleave with many gems scattered across Deluvia to increase its power. The player can also collect the **Mane of Murobrontz** for later use as a reagent for frost spells.

LEVEL 3

The Courtyard. . . The frozen trophies of The Lady are here. You can unfreeze some to gain extra lore knowledge, but unfreeze the wrong one, they will attack you. At the end are the frozen Knights of Freenbrist, very formidable.

LEVEL 4  
The Frostborn defend  
The ice Spectres are other players who have not quite completed the quest, and failed and were turned into wandering souls. Those players that are online that have turned are made aware of you reaching this level and can come to defend this level. Though they lack physical power, they can all together do a lot of damage. One Ice Spectre can do 1 point of frost damage every 10 seconds, 2, can do 2, 3 can do 4, 4 can do 6, 5 can do 16, 6 can do 32, 7 can do 64 \- 7, 8 can do 128  
This level also has some attunement areas where the player can talk to the Ice Spectres, whereas, in normal game play they can not. This allows the Spectres to either lure the player into their ranks, or haunt the player with words. The player must simply get through. If no Ice Spectres are online, this will be simple. This area gets more difficult as time goes on in the world timeline.

LEVEL 5

This is the court of the 5 Frost Goblin Princes. Here the player learns more lore about the Goblin race which to that lore quest and how the 5 Princes were each given as tribute to The Lady from the Goblin King, Aleighgazor who now resides in Gozon, Druvenrog.  
Each court room guards one of 5 possible random entrances to the next level. The other four lead to a maze. Unless they choose the correct answer to the riddle, they are not given the right gate and must randomly choose.  
**Miniztron** \- Goblin Prince 1: Maze of Insanity. The player must choose the right combination to get out and then they are dumped out at Level 4\. The player can get the **Gear of Truth** artifact here  
**Fozgorn** \- Goblin Prince 2: Maze of Paranoia. The player’s misdeeds are broadcast to Frostwyn. The player is then dumped out in Bokmal’s land. The player can get the **Valve of Sanity**  
**Prizlin** \- Goblin Prince 3: Maze of Chaos. The maze is constantly shifting in random order to then be dumped out at the entrance to Hythlodaeus’ domain. The player can get the **Axle of Order**  
**Moffgo** \-  Goblin Prince 4: Maze of Deception. Invisible walls and traps. The player can get the **Lense of Candor.** The player is dumped out at the Goblin Atoll.  
**Sinerzip** \- Goblin Prince 5: Maze of Delusion. Player is brought close to the end of the fortress and can see The Lady of the Snow, but then is dumped out at the entrance. The player can get the **Sextant of Reality**.

From each of the mazes the player can find 2 artifact ruins per maze to decipher the Goblin language.

All of the above rewards can be used to bring back to Gozon and combined to form an ultimate **Automaton with Aleighgazor**. The player can only get one of the artifacts from this quest, so they must find the other parts through other means, such as buying or stealing from other players that have them. The second time through the court rooms, after an artifact is found, the rest are removed as an option, but the hardships still remain.  
If the player guesses the riddle correctly, they will go directly to level 6\. The riddle has to do with Goblin lore, so the player is encouraged to study up by finding the other Goblin refugees across Deluvia before starting this level.

LEVEL 6

The outer chambers. The player begins their temptation down the path of Ice Spectre. They are presented with 10 entrances, one of which is correct. The others are one-way paths out to the wilderness of Frostwyn. In the correct path leads to an open field with 3 icy mastadons which charge down the player. The player must slay them and then enter another room with the mastadon’s keeper, **Mammrooth**. After chiding the player for killing his pets he gives the player an option of 3 doors to enter. They can choose one and when they do, Mammrooth opens one of the wrong doors that leads to the entrance of the fortress. He asks if the player wants to change their answer. If they don’t he fights the player. When he is finally is defeated, before he dies, he offers the key to the right door if the player spares his life, otherwise the key dies with him. If they kill him, they get the skill of mastadon taming but then can never complete the quest. If they  leave him alive, they can get the right door, but Mammrooth will come back later to taunt them.

LEVEL 7 

The Lady of the Snow is waiting on the other side of the door. She is magnificent but frightful in all her icy glory. She asks why the player hadn’t killed Mammrooth and says there will be another chance. She is testing the player. She says she needs a force to raid the dark fiery domain of Necromensus and can offer much power to the player in exchange for their help. If the player has already obtained The Blade of Abhorrence she will enchant it with the cold vortex ability if the player take the path to become part of her army.  
If the player takes the other path, she is mad and leaves the player in the room with snow golems to tend with. 

LEVEL 8   
If the player defeats the snow golems they proceed to part 4 (this eventually leads them out of the quest, never able to complete it. They should have gotten enough treasure and skills to be content )  
If the player agrees to the dark path, they proceed to part 3 with the eventual possibility to complete the whole quest.

### Part 3 \- The Frostborn

The player accepts The Lady of the Snow’s invitation to become a Frostborn, one of her army of Ice Spectres. This army consists of all other players that have come this far. It is a difficult path to finish becoming one, but even more difficult to undo this pact. There are only two known ways to undo becoming a Frostborn; one is to undergo the unborn quest which is the most difficult way (and is the completion of the quest- Part 5), or have a player that is among the corporeal realm go through the quest free all the Frostborn. (this is another epic quest for a player as well).

Whatever class that player has at this point is abandoned and they achieve the class of Frostborn, which is a combination of a frost mage and a death mage, with some unique spells and abilities mixed in.

One ability is to be able to go into ethereal form. This allows them to be invisible to mortals and able to go through solid objects. At first they can only go into this form for short periods, but the more they use this ability, the more it randomly happens to them, until eventually the player is always in this form forever. They are unable to hold physical objects in this form (except for special frost weapons such as the Sword of Abhorrence), but will gain new spells that can be used while in this form. This opens up a whole new world for the player, but also closes down a whole world.

Other restrictions are that The Lady expects you to spend much of your time in Frostwyn. She expects you to come to her aid when beckoned, and she will expect you to train for and participate in the epic battle she has planned with Necromensus and his minions when the time is right. 

The Lady of the Snow has more communication with her acolytes than most deities, especially when her powers are heightened while in Frostwyn.

If a Frostborn goes absent, they may get hunted down by the rest of the Frostborn army which is their duty to do so. AWOL Frostborn are flagged and other Frostborn that capture them, gain extra XP.

TASK 1  
The Tears of Freymiss  
Where Freymiss’ tears fell is marked in the souls of the Frostborn and are their first pilgrimage.  
There are still remnants of her frozen tears here, which never melted and which, when gathered, become the soul of a Frostborn. They must go retrieve one to start receiving their power. When gathered they bring it back to the altar behind The Lady of the Snow’s throne room for a ritual to convert the player to a Frostborn.  
Before the ritual is over, The Lady binds the player to kill either a follower of The Free Spirit Sage, or The Scholar Sage, as she sees them as competition and defilers of the original tears and flowers her sisters and cousins were born from. The player gets access to one new frost spell for each follower they kill and bring the head back to The Lady. Only one is necessary to move onto the next task.

TASK 2  
The Scouting of Doomforge  
Doomforge is the domain of Necromensus and on the opposite end of the world. It is easier for the player to do this while they still retain some corporeal power, as they can use transportation means of mortals to get there. If they haven’t been there before, getting there and finding it is a quest on its own. When the player does finally get there, their ethereal form ability gets lengthened from 5 seconds per day, to 10\. This is pure roleplaying and The Lady only expects whatever information the spectre can and is willing to provide.

TASK 3   
Kill an ice troll warlord.   
Infiltrate Bokmal’s domain to the east in Frostwyn. The player finds an encampment. Once there, they receive an upgrade to their ethereal ability to 20 seconds a day and the spell to call a frost dire wolf to their aid.  
There is much conversation with the warlord and he tries to convince the player of the curse they have with The Lady of the Snow and it would be much better to join the trolls against the gods and learn their own type of shamanic ice magic. The player is given the choice. If they continue the battle with the warlord, they get the **Talisman of Brigningrod**, which gives the highest amount of frost magic protection.   
The player then will start to get weakened physical characteristics but also has the ability to go into ethereal mode twice a day for 20 seconds each. The player is now put onto Bokmal’s enemy list.

TASK 4  
Haunting of Herrothorg  
Herrothorg, the ice prison is a terrible place for prisoners. One of the reasons is the rumors that they are spooked by ghosts. These not just rumors but actually the Frostborn. Herrothorg is a prison colony of New Pallamost, and The Lady despises the ambitious humans. For this she expects her minions to make trouble for the guards and prisoners there. Once they arrive they get \+10 seconds added to their ethereal form, but they will intermittently go in and out of ethereal form if they are in corporeal form.  They also get the spell of **telekinesis**, to move objects that are far away. \<more info needed  here as to how they haunt\>

TASK 5  
Gathering of Frizwhils  
Frizwhils is an old Frostborn general who calls the Gathering to further initiate the acolytes. They are presented with a new spell, **Mullbrufrost Recall**, which allows them to return to Mullbrufrost entrance in an instant. They are given the **Ice Pike** dagger which deals frost damage. Frizwhils explains more about their missions and the player can meet other Frostborn.   
Frizwhils also takes away their corporeal form and they are permanently in ethereal form. Since all Frostborn come to this, it only happens at certain intervals, (once per week?), so the player must find other things to do if they are waiting for this to move onto the next task. The player also gets their own dwelling in the Caves of Griffmourne, a world that normal corporal players cannot get to. In this world, the Frostborn can build freely.  
   
TASK 6  
Maintenance of Mullbrufrost  
The Lady’s fortress needs some expansion and repair. This is also in preparation of a potential invasion by Necromensus. Though Necromensus has much more on his mind, and other goals and enemies, The Lady does feel like he may raid her fortress just to spite her. She is paranoid and hates him, but it is possible.  (Necromensus has a similar acolyte system which makes them mortal enemies of the Frostborn and locked in eventual ethereal battle). The player gets some building ability with certain frost blocks. Frizwhils also directs which areas need to be built. This task gets the player acquainted with the potential war with Necromensus’s empire. This also allows them to now build upon their plot in Griffmourne.

TASK 7  
The Snuffing of the Great Forge  
The Lady does not like questors stealing her artifacts and thawing them and she has it out for Druvenrog and their Great Forge. Fozgorn, one of the Frost Goblin Princes will guide you to Gozon and introduce you to Aleighgazor, the Goblin King. Once here the player will get 10 seconds back that they can choose to go into corporeal form.

Aleighgazor tries to convince you to help him unite all the Goblins in one nation, as they are now spread across the world. This would entail Aleighgazor retracting his tribute of the 5 Princes to The Lady, but in return, he will help her destroy the Great Forge. This ends up becoming its own large quest that a group of players can complete. (Uniting the Goblins is also a large quest.) Once complete, the Great Forge is done, altering the nature of the world.  Once this quest is complete, it is removed from the Frostborn tasks.

TASK 8  
Kidnap one of Necromensus’ 5 daughters  
The Frostborn player is sent again to Doomforge. The Lady of the Snow wants as her captive one, or all of Necromensus’ daughters. They are his most prized possessions so this is difficult.  
She desires this to bring Necromensus to her domain to fight the epic battle, where she will hav e home field advantage of her frost spells and beasts.  
It should be said only 5 players can complete this; perhaps less, as during their quest during the capture or on the return could result in an alternative ending. The final spell is lanumagicor  a teleportation skill to 8 locations across Deluvia

Once these 8 tasks are complete, the player is then pure Frostborn with at least 16 frost spells, invisibility and ability to go through walls, and the ability to instantly teleport to the  locations.  
They now train and do the Lady of the Snow’s bidding in waiting for the epic war against Necromensus.

### Ozymandius

Ozymandius is the lizard king/god on the large equatorial island of Strifftrat Major and the leader of the lizardmen pirates. The lizardmen roam the islands in that region and operate a kidnapping syndicate, where ransom coin is their main source of income. Most captains avoid this small region, as there is little reason to go here anyway.

Ozymandius gained his position through his leadership, vicious prowess in raiding, and most importantly, his immense size. His ancestors have ruled the lizards as a divine right as a demigod. Their culture has it that once signs of aging begin, however, that is a sign that his reign is over, and the lizard people perform regicide and feast on his flesh. This has fostered a tradition of the latest king investing heavily in anti-aging methods to hold onto his throne as long as he can, and delay his demise.

Ozymandius's son Pryomandius, wait for the regicidal Day of Dyziat where he can eat the flesh of his father and take up his throne and rule.

Ozymandius is 1042 years old.

### Brumaltas

The snow beast of the North is Brumaltas. This creature made entirely of snow and held together by frost magic will toss icy snowballs at travelers causing great pain. He makes an appearance on one of the Northern Isle during mid winter and offers unique treasures.

There is one way to defeat Brumaltas and if you haven't guessed it, then you best stay back in Endergeddon Spawn area.

### Bokmal

The chief of a band of frost trolls in the far north that prey off of the occasional traveler searching for the Northern Passage. This band of frost trolls is different in that they have their own written language and are literate, something that Bokmal is proud of. He has secret ambitions to make a nation that trades with the rest of the nation-states of Deluvia, though this is far off

### Lych Lords of Wraithwood

The Lych Lord has lived eons without knowledge of what goes on with the passage of time above. He rules his ancient mausoleum that is deep below the Wraithwood and remains agnostic from the troubles in the overland he once had domain over.\\r\\n\\r\\nHis path into necromancy is unknown as the tomes of this lore are buried in his library. Scholars seek this \<strong\>Necronomicon Library\</strong\> as it would open up knowledge of an undocumented history of the Second Age of when the Lych Lord was once ruler. Adventurers seek his lair for fame and fortune. Followers of necromancy seek the \<strong\>Phylacteron\</strong\>, the amulet that is the source of his power that keeps him animated and powerful enough to defy death. In fact he cannot be killed simply by running him through with a sword of any kind, but by draining his source.\\r\\n\\r\\nNow this corpse of a king walks in shrouds among his undead minions and lonely souls soaking in the deathly powers of the Wraithwood hollows, mostly content to be left alone. He sits on his throne of bones with pallid skin, black hands and sunken anemic face upon which sits his crown. He once rode among the other Undead kings on his pale stead \<strong\>Thaumalatus \</strong\>bringing dread and pestilence to all living things. After the Wars of the Third Age he has retreated to his halls to haunt only those that come close. And coming close is difficult indeed, as the entrance to this lychgate is small and nondescript among the gnarled trees, deep in the Wraithwood. Tellers of tales say that travelers can hear the rumbled playing  of macabre dirges on his pipe organ deep in the putrid soil sending miserable vibes outward.

Artifact: Crown of the Five Kings ( a crown with 5 spikes)

### Saughill Mist

The Observatory of Saughill Mist has been a pilgrimage of many astrologers over the ages. Located in the Riftlands they keep watch over the night skies. This tight-knit brotherhood of astrologers only approve new members when the Red and White moons align. Travelers are always welcomed and offered refuge from the cold winds, if one is able to make it up the thousand step walk to their high outcrop. They will not spill their secrets readily. Their allegiance was once to New Pallamost for whom they were advisors, but that was before the Wars.Now they watch and prophesy only for themselves.  
The Fraternity's main circle is astrology, though they do keep alchemists and enchanters in their midst, for hand-crafting potions and enchantments based upon their astrological knowledge, but all for the solitary goal of watching above and making predictions of things to come. This is also one of the few places to view the kingdoms of Kapasia, the floating land masses above.

Hollow Grove Guardian

### World Guard info

The whole world is protected against building.

Towns are protected against building, but certain areas can be rented or bought. This priority level does not give them permission to build in greater Song Tide

NPC areas outside of towns can never be built in except by game masters (GM)

Some players will be granted permission to build in greater Song Tide, but not in any of the areas above. They will be granted one small plot. Size TBD. 

# The History of New Pallamost  (The Old Order)

The history of New Pallamost is as old as the Third Age. When the Age of Gods ended and The Age of Men rose one of the Twelve Sages,  The Sage The Cleric came upon the land that he found good. He set up a shrine to Pallas, son of Sifaneus of the Deluvic faith. Over the years, pilgrims would come to this island of Pallamost (meaning *Greatest Pallatia* ) and a town was founded. The Sage The Cleric then left to find more mysteries of Deluvia, where Kaln Azernath, one of the founding pilgrims built the town that would now be called Pallamost.   
The Pallatian Clerics, some of the most devout pilgrims founded their order and are now known to be the oldest order in Deluvia.  
Pallamost grew quickly, as the beings known as men were able to replicate much and generations changed quickly. Kaln’s grave is still in the main cemetery, and each of his descendants would reign as a king. Kaln would be known, retroactively, as the first Azernath King. 

Here is a list of events in the the Azernath Dynasty

The 12 Sages, of which I am one, were birthed from the Omphalos, straight out of that gash in Deluvia and spread in 12 directions. The Sages procreated with the children of Gods and some of their children were demigods, and others were mortals. It was Sage \- The Cleric, that came upon the mountain of Keed and met the god Pallas. There she progenerated with Pallas and all of their children were Pallatian and founded the city of Pallamost. It was many januul before it was Kaln Azernath, the devout pilgrim, that started the Pallatian Order and became the first Pallatian King.

* His son, Jom Azernath inherited the kingdom and started work on the Pallatian Cathedral to honor and worship Pallas, which would come to be the most impressive temple in our land.  
* His son, Kropeth Azernath inherited the kingdom; expanded the city and his castle greatly.  
* His son, Kaln Azernath II inherited the kingdom. During his reign, the discovery of the Mines of Didolmauz was made which allowed for new ores to be discovered and made into new building materials.  
* His son, Riddik Azernath inherited the kingdom. This period was of great peace and a treaty with The Kingdom of the Wood making them friends and allies.  
* His son, Kaln Azernath II inherited the kingdom. The Pallatian Court is formed a group of 12 high advisor-knights from across the now expanded kingdom and his leadership council.  
* His son, Kaln Azernath IV inherited the kingdom. The first colony formed at Brinsbik, the cathedral main apse is finished, The Legion army is formed to help keep peace from pirates and other threats on the Long Sea.  
* His son, Jom Azernath II inherited the kingdom. Many more colonies formed including, Sharniss, Pletiak, Cusi, Dormchevril, and Brillgrig. Jom Azernath II declares himself Emperor of Deluvia and makes Pallamost as the Capital City to the disapproval of the other kingdoms.  
* His son, Tillik Azernath inherited the kingdom. The Pallatian navy is formed and the Legion goes to sea to keep the interests of Pallmost intact. New treaties are made with the Outer Rim factions. Pallamost never had a good navy, but was rather known for its land army.  
* His son, Tillik Azernath II inherited the kingdom. The cathedral finishes the central dome, the Festival of Dolstide is established to celebrate all that is great about Pallas and Pallamost and the nearly finished cathedral. He labels himself as "He who grasps the world", and invests in the spiritual realm and art over the temporal realm.  
* His son, Kaln Azernath V inherited the kingdom. The cathedral is considered complete and the Grand Tourney of Deluvia is established as part of the Festival of Dolstide. Pallamost is considered the capital of Deluvia, though most of the Outer Rim do not recognize this.  
* His son, Xandrius inherited the kingdom.  The Battle of Brinsbik starts when the colony revolts and Xandrius  dispels the rebellion with the force of The Legion and an army of mages. The Tome of Grimney is discovered ushering in a new era of magic and arcane knowledge. The Iconologia was another such book added to the collection.  
  * **The Book of Conquests** is written  
  * **The Tome of Grimney** is discovered  
  * **Iconologia** book is written  
  * The Pallamostians are all about their books of knowledge  
* His son, Kaln Azernath VI inherited the kingdom. Construction begins on the Library of Xandrius to house the Tome of Grimney and the history and knowledge of the empire.  
* Swightmich Bellafrok \- The first non-Azernath to be Emperor, but one of the Pallatian Legion to rule as a military leader to quell all the rebellions happening across the empire. The Legion grows to its strongest and largest. New technologies in seafaring are developed.  
* Kaln Azernath VII grandson of Kaln Azernath VI takes back the kingdom. The Azernaths are returned to the throne after a civil war, with the mages aligned with the king turning the tide of the battle. Part of the Pallatian Legion breaks off to form a military colony in the Outer Rim under Swithmich Bellafrok’s son, of the same name.  
* His son, Lornis Azernath inherited the kingdom. He added the Pallatian statues to the four corners of the Cathedral. New farming techniques are developed.  
* His son, Kaln Azernath VIII inherited the kingdom. This is the largest that the empire will ever be.   
* His son, Kazer  Azernath inherited the kingdom.  Kazer allies with dark forces in the Kingdom of the Wood in hopes of expanding the empire even further. He ends up resigning in disgrace and going into exile.  Many more small and uncontrolled colonies founded. Kazer Azernath refers to himself as Emperor of Deluvia even after his expulsion.  
* Kaln Axernath VIII's other son, Tillik Azernath III resumes the throne. After many rebellions, the empire shrinks. A faction of The Kingdom of the Wood attacks the capital causing a rift in the Treaty of Dolstide. 500 januul have passed since the founding of Pallamost.  
* His son, Jom Azernath III inherits the kingdom.  The Glypics, which Pallamost had as slaves to build the cathedral, the castle, and mine finally revolt causing a great war that will last several generations  
* His son, Preestrom Azernath inherited the kingdom. He makes an alliance with Bellafrok’s kingdom in the south to come back and help with the rebellion. Other mercenaries are contracted. Half of Pallamost destroyed.  
* Killmyfis Bellafrok/Kaln Azernath IX \- Joint ruling between the Bellafroks and Azernaths to dispel the Formoris.  
* Kaln Azernath X \- Kaln the Great, as he is known now, brings in alliances from across Deluvia to quell the rebellion, and new friends from the Outer Rim including the Dworvin kingdoms.  Druvenrog founded as a colony by the Nemedi and Formoris.  
  This new colony of Druvenrog allies with their old oppressor Pallamost  
* Jom Azernath IV \- The Great Deluge occurs setting the world in upheaval and half under water. 90% of the kingdom is underwater and only the mountain top, luckily where the kingdom castle and cathedral are, is saved. Most Pallamostans leave upon the Long Sea to escape. This also puts a temporary end to the War. The city is now called New Pallamost to indicate this new era.   
* Dux Joyzil, the populist, only half Azernath blood, Dux comes to power to try to calm and join the kingdom back together. The King’s son, is lost at sea and his daughter, princess Franday is born and is attained to help Dux Joyzil rule and keep the kingdom seem intact.  
* The King is ill and has appointed his adopted son Ayrcheck to make decisions in the hopes of saving what is left of the kingdom. Magic and religion seem to be lost. New threats from The Outer Rim, Demons, Gargoyles, Druvenrog and others are pressuring the queen. The Bellafroks want the throne, Jom Azernath IV’s grandson wants the throne, and other outside upstarts also do. The King’s court has a lot to contend with and this is the current time of Deluvia.  
* I, Vorishba, observed this kingdom from afar, occasionally receiving pilgrims to my humble hut that sought wisdom for Pallamost. As it is now New Pallamost is only a shadow of its once great glory.  
*   
  This is the current time of Deluvia

New Pallamost is the capital city of Deluvia. This term only meant something in ages past and currently, and though many regard the city for its former glory, the seat of rule is currently nowhere.  Power waned after the Wars of the Third Age (The Deluvian Wars) due to many factors, but one being the loss of free labor through Gargoyle enslavement (their freedom being granted through the Truce of Gurgulalon, the armistice to end the war). The rising seas also caused much loss of land for them driving them back to the islands they currently inhabit. Mainly, they have not kept up on technological research and are resting on their laurels of what they consider their "right" to rule by inheritance from the gods.  
They follow their patron demi-god Pallatia, the hero of the Gigantomachian Ballads, an epic poem. Pallatia is a son of Sifaneus of the Deluvic Faith. The Temple to Pallatia, is a one of the largest in the realm, meant to impress all pilgrims to this region. Every year, on the Queen's birthday, which coincides with the lining up of the season of Dolstide, there is the Festivus Drans Pallatia, which Pallatia's battle is reenacted and the children dress as the young Pallatia. The newest members are knighted to the Pallatian Court on this day and the Queen's Grand Tournament is held. For this whole week the city is enlivened with celebration.  
New Pallamost still holds the judicial seat of the Central Kingdoms region and the Independent Kingdoms occasionally bring matters to the court. The central banking system for the realm is here, the best art galleries, museums and gardens can be perused. There is still a vibrant industry, though they are quickly losing out to House Storm King.  
They still like to speak of the years of glory and the grandeur they once had. The Queen Redfayne Joyzil speaks of his victorious battles of the past to anyone that comes to listen in his court, but the waning Queen is reduced to little more than puppet government for a once, vast kingdom and powerful Lord. Most will admit the technocrats of the Northern Islands now compete for power. He rules as head of his Pallatian Court, 12 elite warrior kings from certain rigid bloodlines. Much of the land holdings of the court had be lost after the wars. Their border shrinks daily.  
Queen Redfayne assumed control of the realm when her King, Dux Joyzil died in the wars of the Third Age. Many thought her kingdom would crumble. She has managed to keep control with the help of her court.  
Despite this, New Pallamost remains the culture hub of the central kingdoms and most any good or service can be bought and desire met; passage to any port can be found and people and entertainment of most varieties located.  
Points of interest are the docks where the shipyards lie. Goods are constantly being shipped in and out, by sea and by the new mode of transportation: air. The market is one of the best for the variety and luxury of goods. The restaurants and taverns are the talk of Deluvia. The Queen's Palace is not to be missed. The [Grand Tournament](http://steamfront.net/deluvia-grand-tourney/) is held each year as part of the Festival of Dolstide  and The Queen awards a coveted prize. A gargoyle statue, gifted by the Gargoyles as a peace tribute is on view. The Library of Xandris the largest collection of knowledge and scholars to be sought. The Temple of Pallamost is where the Queen's Champion is awarded at the Festival of Dolstide. The temple is also the destination of many pilgrims of the Paladin Aura. There are parks and gardens and much for travelers to see.

Druvenrog has many secrets as they are investing in new technologies such as airships and the Ichor from the Deep. Their newest idea is to pump Ichor from the Deep into huge mechanized Golems. # Other Kingdoms

### Cult of the Holy Dread

There are many vile and horrible things in Deluvia, but one is the rising influence of the Cult of the Holy Dread.\\r\\n\\r\\nThey reside in the outcast camps far in the edges of the southern lands but no one knows for sure. Any troops sent to return with their bounty has never come back. The Troops could have been lost to the Cliffs of Sangor, for which many believe you must sail through to find their encampment, inducted into the Cult's ranks, or slaughtered by them.\\r\\n\\r\\nOne reason they are so despised is that they lure in the young men of Deluvia promising power and fortune, but their religion is a deceptive one. Once they have brainwashed a new acolyte, they have become part of the brain-, hive-minded, bloodlust horde that raids ships with menacing force. If only they didn\\'t have some sway and influence in their messaging to gain new followers.\\r\\n\\r\\nStay tuned to this post to know more of their dreadful acts committed in the dank bowels of their hideout. If this reporter can continue to send out missives without being caught, we can expose them and hunt them down.

### Hythlodaeus.

Meet Hythlodaeus. Or maybe you would rather not as he is the ruler of a small domain among the Southern Islands where hostility and destruction abound and everything is turned on its head.  
His labyrinthine underground keep is where he's spent the last 3000 years setting traps and malevolent puzzles for any traveler coming to greet him.  
This trickster, the annals say, was responsible for pitting the dragons against each other and starting the Great Deluge for which our world is known. It is For this great and honorable warriors sought revenge. None have been heard from again.  
Other, more industrious rogues, have sought to steal his **ammulekrom**, the secret nonsense language which is the source for his chaotic powers.  
His child is the beast Zalrumurlith which guards over the Tantalon Remis Stone Temple of Despise.

Necromensus as his wife, Embreas are building up their powers to return the gods back to their once greatness.

### Crimson Patriarch of the Duravian Empire,

Long before he was the Crimson Patriarch of the Duravian Empire, Ren\\'Aroz was known as Renwald the Rogue. Or, rather, he had hoped he would be considered as such, but Renwald was not per say the best at what he did. Born into an elvish family of hunters, Renwald was likely the least useful. His talents as a silver tongue and a proper communicator was all but wasted on those who considered silence and the shadows as their only ways to survive. When asked of his time before finding Necromensus, he would often laugh about it, shrugging it off like it was simply another life. And, when asked how he found his calling as a demon, he often regales the commoner with a well spun tale, that goes something like this.\\n\\n\\"It was a warm spring night, the entire clan was out either hunting or gathering for the large feast to be held at sunrise. I was tasked, along with many of my bretherin, to bring back a stag, or deer; something to appease the elders. However, I was never one for hunting exactly, and I was probably more likely to end up shooting a friend or relative crouching in a bush faster than I\\'d be able to hit a moving deer. In fact, and I'm not exactly proud of this, but I can honestly say, once or twice I almost did. But, this night was a little different. I had wandered perhaps very far from my village, and found myself lost way beyond recognition. I tried looking around for my village, and at the first sign of light and life, I sprinted towards it, barely missing several bear traps also hidden amongst the brush. What I came upon was not my village, but rather a glowing shrine, one of which I've only heard about among my tribes various legends. Of course I went towards it, and the second I touched it, everything came to life. The large dark stone circle standing resolute and cold in the dark woods, began to resonate with an eerie purple hue. I wanted to step back, but I heard a voice calling from beyond the void, ebbing me towards it. Against my better judgement, though I know now it was the best decision of my life, I ended up walking right into it. After several splitting headaches, a new voice in my mind and in my heart, and a mind boggling transformation that began at my head, and ended with a new tail, I eventually wandered back to my village, to be quickly chased out as some sort of invader. After all that madness, I sought answers starting with that shrine. Something in my mind guided me back to it and that lead to my first correspondence with Necromensus. He told me about demon culture, how my new life was there, blah blah blah, and he told me to step through his dimension, to come through into a strong colony that needed a voice. So, that's how I got here, in Duravia.\\"\\n\\nAfter reaching his new home, greeted by his fellow demons, he quickly found his talent put to use as Necromensus had said. Ren\\'Aroz, as his ember told him to be called now, quickly aided him in rising up the ranks of the political forces in the growing underground demon coven. Though many demons Patriarchs have come to power with the knowledge of war, and glory from many battles, Ren\\'Aroz has managed to maintain peace, and continues to grow his colony into an empire: The Duravian Empire. # The History of the Kingdom of the Wood

The Kingdom of the Wood, is a realm that time forgot, and is still imbued with much of the manifestation of the Gods and Goddesses. Rich with mega flora and fauna, the waters teem with life, and the soils are abundant and fertile.

The faerie-folk and ents were the first to inhabit this region, but after the expulsion from the torrential Deluge, many new refugees have come seeking shelter under the great tree, **Drasilissigeaunt**. This tree, which was a gift to the faerie-demigod, King of the Wood, when he was young, as a wedding gift from his mother, Nemistri, one of the great goddesses of old. The rich spring in which he planted the sapling, caused it to grow high and strong over the eons. ncThe faerie-folk and ents built their civilization in the branches of this ancient Sylvan Oak. 

The blessing of Nemistri have kept this realm sacred and protected for so long, that the citizens feel safe and are unaware of the Rotwood Blight  creeping out of the Corrupted Wraithwood, their close neighbor.

Most of the Kingdom of the Wood is wild. Their existence is bounded by the wilderness, by the unyielding darkness of ancient woods. Most of the Wood is the place where most beings are not supposed to be, and dangerous to most. It is natural and it is free. The forest hid all manner of danger, but it is where he had to roam. The trees can hide more than deadly creatures and lawless men however, magic and madness can lie in wait, shall we ever stray too far from the path. 

## Urd Drasil

Another realm that is quite influential that goes back to the beginning of the Age of Mortals is The Kingdom of the Wood. The Wood, is where the goddess Nemistri settled. She is half god, half mortal but is still one of the most powerful deities in Deluvia. The Wood is steeped in magic and most all of its inhabitants practice magery to some degree. 

Nemistri has given the day-to-day ruling of The Wood, particularly the center region, called Fecundia, to her son, Urd Drasil so that she can about keeping magic intact in her realm while magic is under threat. Urd Drasil's father, **Rattelhob**, another demigod, gifted a pet to Urd Drasil, The **Therion Stag**, what become a large megolosaurus giganteus, that is one of the mega fauna that gives Fecundia is power of growth and fertility. 

In the center of Fecundia is also the well of **Aqua Vitae**, the magical waters the flow below Fecundia and give it most of its fertile powers. This well, called the **well of Faenkra**, is the access point to the waters and is ruled over by Urd Drasil.

When Urd Drasil chose a mate, he chose a human mortal from the town of **Rivenward (Gwelftshire)**, just down the hill from the Well of Fenkra. As a wedding gift, Nemistri gifted Urd Drasil, and his new wife, Yore, a golden sapling called Drasil. You see, *Drasil* means Wood in the old Deluvic tongue. *Urd* means Ruler, so Urd Drasil's name is the mortal tongue literally means Wood King. 

Because Yore drank from Faenkra, she outlived all of her mortal family and counterparts, and Drasil grew to be hundreds of feet tall and the home to Urd Drasil and his court. The mortal town of Rivenward regarded Yore very highly, since she was born there and each januul had a festival called Yore's Festival, in which she always tried to attend. Urd Drasil was jealous of the affection the town gave her and kept her locked in the top of the Great Tree Drasil, the God Treee. He expected all of the praise from the mortals in Fecundia for himself.

It was one januul during Yore's Festival that Yore had hanged herself from her neck from the highest branch of Drasil because of the sorrow of being separated from her people, and the petty jealousy of her husband. When the people of Rivenward found about this they started to hate UrdDrasil and a dark cloud hung over Rivenward and much of Fecundia. People referred to the Great Tree Drasil as (Yorishwood) Yore's Gallow from then on.

In Fecundia, the residents desire to stay in touch with ***Asil***, the spiritual energy of a particular place or member of nature. Asil can be translated to Nature Spririts.

Faendrasi translates into the “The Way of the Nature Spirits”

To them the fox is the messenger spirit of Nemistri. Purification is a prime aspect of all rituals in Faendrasi religion. It exists to find balance between nature and the races and the gods. This counteracts the effects of pollution, which is considered an obstruction to the flow of life and the blessing from the Asil.

The residents of Faekundia are called **Kunddrasil**, *Kund* meaning child and *Drasil* meaning wood. They are Children of the Wood

The Asil also love music and to be entertained. The bard class has many songspells that work to bring favor from the Asil. Music can be used to speak to the spirits of the forest.

The three key aspects of Fecunda are Balance, Purity and Transformation

Other things:

The Wolf Walkers are a druid clan in Fecundia

**Drasilissigeaunt** is located in the region called **The Valley of the Moon**. (Mynith Vale) The old goddess Meena, guarded the valley for millenia, until she took part in the Wars of the Second Age, and she has not been seen since. She had blessed Nemistri to be the guardian of the Mynith Vale until her return., part of Faekundia where the waters lead. A path leads down into the valley on it’s north side from other small towns and winds through the heath and approaching Drasillissigeaunt from the north, crossing the River Sylvene and up to the Elden Gate.   
Drasil is home to many races, and refuge to The Faefolk, which inhabit the interior of the truck, inside the branches and upon the branches.

The **River Mnimimor** flows through the center of this land and around the tree and holds the memories of this land.

The FaeFolk are a divine proto-species. They are all children of Nemistri and followers of the moon.

Once one enters the Elden Gate, they enter the many towns of the Drasil. The core of the civilization of the Faefolk. The moons give power from above, and the Faenkra fountain gives power from below. All of the Fae in Drasil live in harmony and with and among each other, but there are certain Districts and some have different percentage of habitants.

The first level or Thenchrios is a market district. The path from the Elden gate goes south and is flanked by shops of magic trinkets, bakeries, flower shops. Metal objects, are forbidden in The Faewood, and they corrode and rust almost immediately. Wood armor and weapons are fine. The Faefolk are powerful magic wielders, so conventional weapons are not that common, but a few shops of weapons and armor might be found, as some Anthorans have found their home in Drasil and deal in such goods.    
After going south for a bit, the path goes left and right. The leftward way leads to Underthenchrios, and the Fabbersgrin Alley to the east and Morelinn Lanes, down paths to the west.  This beginning area of Thenchrios, though cute and wonderful, is more practical. Though the Faefolk are wary of other races encroaching on their lands, they still see the value of not scaring off Anthoran and other races as allies, and therefore try to keep the entrance welcoming.   
The original path curves west and leads into the main atrium of the Central Hall of Cooriechrios (Referred to as The Coorie).  There is the crest of Drasil on the floor which is recessed leading down to the main fountain of Faenkra, which pilgrim pay tribute. Many lanterns hang from inside the chamber. A large Thimberbough spirals up inside of the Central Hall to lead to upper levels. On the eastern side of the Central Hall is Ticker of Tuuneth the gift of Boonstone the Gnome crafter to Drasil. Boonstone is one of the great holographic tinkers in Faewood and now resides in his own workshop out in the wild.

## Witheryn

Part of the Kingdom of the Wood is Witheryn, so named because  it’s blighted necrosis and dying realm. Witheryn encompasses the dead tree Torilkaew and the huge expanse of the Wraithwood

## Wraithwood (Forest of Bones)

Wraithwood is a large island to the far western edge The Kingdom of the Wood that has been overtaken by the undead and forsaken by Fecundia.  The undead forces rising there are because of the waning power of nemistri and the Therion Stag, and the pettiness of UrdDrasil

UrdDrasil, seeing the power of Fenkra and of the Therion Stag, assumed there could be even more power. At first he told himself this was for his people, but after he stewed upon this idea for many years he eventually sawed off the antlers of the Therion Stag to investigate and harness their powers further. This was a mistake, for what really happened was the blessing spell over Fecundia was lessened and the dark forces of the undead, which were waiting at the edge moved in to suck the rich life for their own power. This is UrdDrasil’s secret and he keeps it such from the rest of the woodfolk. Many of the western edges of the kingdom succumbed to the undead without notice. The woodfolk directly around Drasil were safe because of Fenkra. UrdDrasil kept this secret out of embarrassment. When his mother, nemistri, confronted him, he tricked her and bound her to be locked away in Torilkaew. The curse of Torilkaew sapped nemistri’s powers even dragging UrdDrasil’s kingdom further into decline. It is now a battle of life and death and the edge of Fecundia seem to shrink each day.   
UrdDrasil must be convinced to turn his ways in order to restore The Wood’s power to withstand the dark forces of the Druvenrog empire in the east, or Necromensus’ demon army in the south.

Parents of the KudDrasil call the Wraithwood the Forbidden Forest and tell scary tales to keep them from entering.

There names are now, **Elkesommer**, **Bamphomede**, **Hythlodaeus**, **The Black Father**

They were jealous and all thought they had a right to it.They warred against each other and against their mother so that they could have complete control/ The Ancient Beast **Groddifyth** brought the Four into a dark pact of dominion and the false promise of control of the kingdom.

The Ancient Beast Groddifyth lay deep beneath Fecundia awaiting his chance to lay his revenge upon is half-sister Nemistri. He is the bastard son of Seydna and Grifth the Abomination. After his birth he was soon hidden away from the gods as his parents were ashamed of him; but in him lay great power that he did not even know. He lay far beneath Fecundia, disgraced of his being and with hatred of his sister Nemistri for her dominion over the realm.  
Then he discovered the bitterroot of **Nihlheeg,** part of her hibernating tail that he nourished himself for eons with. He grew strong and learned the magic of death.   
When it came time for Nemistri to inherit her throne to her 5 sons, Groddifyth, their uncle caused dissent among them. It was Nemistri’s plan, to bequeath the kingdom to her favored son, Urd. Groddifyth knew of this and planted an evil seed in his nephews’ mind of jealousy and treachery. He convinced them that in order to regain control of the throne, they, all four, must accept a pact of the bitter root of Nihlheeg to gain the power to overcome the life magic of their Mother.

### Queen Maz

Queen Maz is the Queen of the fairy folk of Barrows, She is part of the Kingdom of the Wood empire and rests below ground in the large numinous mound of dirt among her people. Though small in stature, these folk burrow underground and mine glowstone which is used in the capital of Yore's Gallow.

Queen Maz is a benevolent ruler but is extremely xenophobic to visitors, especially those with the Y chromosome. In fact it is the females of her own realm which dominate and the males who perform the labor functions, serving the females.

The Barrow Lands is a glowstone mining area in a doline in the mountain, as well as known for profuse growth of the poppy on the hills on top. This is the source of the Barrow Folk's sleep magic and time magic. Time in the barrow is much slower than time outside of it and visitors often think they are staying days, when they in fact are staying years.

The Barrow Lands are also plagued by a pesky dirt wyrm named Heeg. His tunneling through the depths of dirt under The  Barrow Lands caused great tremors and problems for their mines until a truce was struck and Queen Maz now offers tribute once a year, of fresh meat in a ceremony in the Heeg's Chamber. This has made the Heeg slow and fat and sleepy and he no longer bothers the Barrow Folk, but does insist upon the sacrifice of a few of her people. She has instead entrapped travelers to her barrow, which are seekers of the poppy and put them in sleep stasis until the Heegs feeding, so she no longer needs to give up her own folk. She still feels guilty about this murderous contract and is looking for a way out.

Though the fairy folk lack might, they are crafty and pesky in numbers against their occasional enemy.  Their sleep and time magic, which is not well known outside the barrow can be powerful. When allied with the rest of the Kingdom of Wood, their organic magic together becomes quite formidable.
